<td style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 299.85pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0pt; PADDING-TOP: 0pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-top-alt: 0.5000pt solid windowtext; mso-border-left-alt: none; mso-border-bottom-alt: 0.5000pt solid windowtext; mso-border-right-alt: 0.5000pt solid windowtext" valign="top" width="399">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">搜查者检定获得2点附加成功</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p></td></tr></table>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">当你隐藏的物品体积超过你自身体积一半时，你隐藏物品检定的所有成功数减半</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">，然后计算难度修正</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">当你隐藏的物品体积超过你自身体积时，你隐藏物品检定自动失败。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">但是当你拥有任何类似</font>”你可以将体积X以下的XX物品藏在身上”时，则你可以无视上述体积要求和对应的体积修正。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">===========================================================================================================</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">求生</font>(Survival)：在户外生存的技能，包括寻觅食料、栖息处所、避免野兽的袭击等，还有对抗毒素和疾病，以及追踪目标的能力。</span></b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">常见用法和对应专业：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">自然环境生存：感知</font>+求生（野外求生）</span></b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">本技能可追迹、在野外打猎、带领队伍安全穿越冰原、辨识附近是否住有枭头熊、预测天气、或避开流沙等自然危险等。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">动作：可变。单独的一次生存检定可能需要数个小时或者一整天。用来寻找足迹的生存检定至少需要一个整轮动作，并且有可能会更长。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">在野外求生时，你要为每一件事分别进行检定，通常在野外行动时，包括以下行为需要检定：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<td style="BORDER-TOP: windowtext 1pt solid; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 98.65pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0pt; PADDING-TOP: 0pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-top-alt: 0.5000pt solid windowtext; mso-border-left-alt: none; mso-border-bottom-alt: 0.5000pt solid windowtext; mso-border-right-alt: 0.5000pt solid windowtext" valign="top" width="131">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">难度</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p></td>

<td style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; BORDER-RIGHT: windowtext 1pt solid; WIDTH: 107.85pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: windowtext 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0pt; PADDING-TOP: 0pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-border-top-alt: 0.5000pt solid windowtext; mso-border-left-alt: none; mso-border-bottom-alt: 0.5000pt solid windowtext; mso-border-right-alt: 0.5000pt solid windowtext" valign="top" width="143">
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">持续时间半速移动</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p></td></tr></table>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">强韧豁免检定：耐力</font>+求生（自我保护）</span></b><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">本项目一般都是针对</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">自身的毒素或者疲劳等情况下进行的豁免检定。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">追踪：感知</font>+求生（追踪）</span></b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">你可以追踪目标的踪迹。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">动作：无需动作。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">使用：追踪他人</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">在追踪时，每追踪</font>2000米，则需要进行一次感知+生存（追踪）检定，若成功方可继续追踪，否则追踪宣告失败。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">同时，由</font>ST判定，每当所追踪的踪迹变为难以辨认，比如被其他踪迹覆盖，刻意抹去，踪迹后退，模糊不清，必须再重新做一次感知+生存（追踪）检定。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">一般情况下，踪迹只会留在地面上，所以你在追踪时，只能停留在地面上。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">一个飞行的生物很难留下踪迹。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">当你进行追踪时，你的基础移动速度下降一半。若你不下降你的基础移动速度，则你追踪检定的成功数减半。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">你在追踪时，根据以下情况调节你追踪的</font>DC：</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">===========================================================================================================</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">白刃</font>(Weaponary)： 
从刀剑到棍棒、枪、矛等等的使用技能。</span></b><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(0,0,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">常见用法和对应专业：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">白刃攻击：由于白刃武器自己对应的</font>”物品分类”所以，我们将专业也对应一一分类到对应的专业中。</span></b><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">使用长剑进行白刃攻击：力量</font>+白刃（长剑）</span></b><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">使用重剑进行白刃攻击：力量</font>+白刃（重剑）</span></b><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">使用突刺剑进行白刃攻击：力量</font>+白刃（突刺剑）</span></b><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">使用舞扇进行白刃攻击：力量</font>+白刃（扇子）</span></b><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">具体的相关规则请去</font>”战斗规则”查询。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">攻击特定部位：白刃攻击：力量</font>+白刃（攻击特定部位）</span></b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">这个专业非常特殊，因为其并不增加你的</font>DP，也不参与相关的检定，而是改为忽略1点攻击特定部位减值。并且该专业可以同时与其他专业生效。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">如：你进行力量</font>+白刃（长剑 
攻击特定部位）的攻击，使用长剑攻击目标的眼睛，则你不仅可以获得专业”长剑”带来的1DP专业加值，同时忽略攻击目标眼睛带来的1点特定部位减值。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">特殊的是：有一些能力或者资源让你专业加值从</font>1DP变为其他DP，这种情况，不会影响”攻击特定部位”专业。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">白刃</font></span></b><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">瞄准：</font></span></b><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">这个专业非常特殊，因为其并不增加你的</font>DP，也不参与相关的检定，而是让你在进行</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">白刃</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">攻击</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">时</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">，更快地进行瞄准。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">当你进行</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">白刃</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">瞄准时，你第一轮的瞄准视为已经瞄准了</font>2轮，这意味着你第一轮的瞄准轮数+1。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">需要注意的是，你只有第一轮的瞄准会变为瞄准</font>2轮，不会影响后续的瞄准。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">特殊的是：有一些能力或者资源让你专业加值从</font>1DP变为其他DP，这种情况，不会影响”</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">白刃</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">瞄准</font>”专业。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">白刃格挡：这是一个防御行为，无需检定。</font></span></b><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">这个专业非常特殊，因为其并不增加你的</font>DP，而是改为当你使用白刃技能值进行”白刃格挡防御”时，给你再额外提供1点格挡防御。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">特殊的是：有一些能力或者资源让你专业加值从</font>1DP变为其他DP，这种情况，本专业提供的额外格挡防御也从1点变为相应的数值。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">===========================================================================================================</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p><!--EndFragment--></div>
